Source Code

This is a reconstructed version of Luminary 130, the initial AGC program released in November 1969 for the Apollo 13 LM. Three more releases followed before the flown revision was finally manufactured in February 1970.

This reconstruction was created from a previous transcription of the original listing of Luminary 131, combined with Luminary memo #129 which describes the small difference between the Luminary 130 and 131. The reconstructed source code was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed for Luminary 130 in drawing 2021152G.

In this source code, program comments from the original (Luminary 131) code are prefixed with '#', while those added later by the Virtual AGC project are prefixed with '##'. 

021192,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
021193,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
021194,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of the reconstructed source code for Luminary 130.
021195,000005:                                                                                                  ##              This was the original program released for the Apollo 13 LM,
021196,000006:                                                                                                  ##              although several more revisions would follow. It has been
021197,000007:                                                                                                  ##              reconstructed from a listing of Luminary 131, from which it
021198,000008:                                                                                                  ##              differs on only two lines in P70-P71. The difference is
021199,000009:                                                                                                  ##              described in detail in Luminary memo #129, which was used
021200,000010:                                                                                                  ##              to perform the reconstruction. This file is intended to be a
021201,000011:                                                                                                  ##              faithful reconstruction, except that the code format has been
021202,000012:                                                                                                  ##              changed to conform to the requirements of the yaYUL assembler
021203,000013:                                                                                                  ##              rather than the original YUL assembler.
021204,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 496-618
021205,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
021206,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
021207,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 05/15/03 RSB.   Began transcribing.
021208,000018:                                                                                                  ##              12/01/03 RSB.   Entered/corrected the previously-missing code from
021209,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              the bottom of p. 595 using a replacement scan
021210,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              provided by Gary Neff.
021211,000021:                                                                                                  ##              05/14/05 RSB    Corrected website reference above.
021212,000022:                                                                                                  ##              2010-10-25 JL   Fixed p583 page number.
021213,000023:                                                                                                  ##              2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.
021214,000024:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-06 RSB  Page numbers now agree with those on the
021215,000025:                                                                                                  ##                              original harcopy, as opposed to the PDF page
021216,000026:                                                                                                  ##                              numbers in 1701.pdf.
021217,000027:                                                                                                  ##              2017-01-28 RSB  WTIH -> WITH.
021218,000028:                                                                                                  ##              2017-02-24 RSB  Proofed comment text using octopus/ProoferComments.

021226,000036:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021227,000037: 
021228,000038:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021229,000039: 
021230,000040:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021231,000041:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021232,000042: 
021233,000043:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021234,000044: 
021235,000045:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021236,000046:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021237,000047:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021238,000048:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021239,000049: 
021240,000050:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021241,000051: 
021242,000052:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021243,000053: 
021244,000054:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021245,000055: 
021246,000056:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021247,000057:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021248,000058:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021249,000059:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021250,000060:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021251,000061:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021252,000062:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021253,000063:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021254,000064:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021255,000065:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021256,000066: 
021257,000067:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021258,000068: 
021259,000069:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021260,000070:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021261,000071: 
021262,000072:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021263,000073: 
021264,000074:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021265,000075: 
021266,000076:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021267,000077: 
021268,000078:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021269,000079: 
021270,000080:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021271,000081: 
021272,000082:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021273,000083: 
021274,000084:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
021275,000085: 
021276,000086:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021277,000087: 
021278,000088:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
021279,000089: 
021280,000090: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021281,000091: 
021282,000092: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021283,000093: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021284,000094: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021285,000095: 
021286,000096: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

021694,000504:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021695,000505: 
021696,000506:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021697,000507:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021698,000508:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021699,000509: 
021700,000510:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021701,000511: 
021702,000512:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021703,000513:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021704,000514:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021705,000515:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021706,000516: 
021707,000517:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021708,000518: 
021709,000519:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021710,000520: 
021711,000521:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021712,000522:

021783,000593:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021784,000594:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021785,000595: 
021786,000596:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021787,000597:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021788,000598: 
021789,000599:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021790,000600: 
021791,000601:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021792,000602:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021793,000603: 
021794,000604:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021795,000605: 
021796,000606:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021797,000607:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021798,000608: 
021799,000609:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021800,000610: 
021801,000611:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021802,000612:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021803,000613:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021804,000614: 
021805,000615:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -

022003,000813:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
022004,000814:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022005,000815: 
022006,000816:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022007,000817:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022008,000818: 
022009,000819:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022010,000820: 
022011,000821:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
022012,000822:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
022013,000823: 
022014,000824:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022015,000825: 
022016,000826:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
022017,000827:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
022018,000828: 
022019,000829:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022020,000830: 
022021,000831:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
022022,000832:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
022023,000833:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
022024,000834:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
022025,000835: 
022026,000836:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
022027,000837:                                                                                                  #        
022028,000838:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
022029,000839:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
022030,000840: 
022031,000841:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022032,000842: 
022033,000843:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
022034,000844:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
022035,000845:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
022036,000846: 
022037,000847:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022038,000848: 
022039,000849:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM

022041,000851:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022042,000852: 
022043,000853:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM

022230,001040:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022231,001041:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022232,001042: 
022233,001043:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022234,001044:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
022235,001045: 
022236,001046:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022237,001047: 
022238,001048:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022239,001049: 
022240,001050:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022241,001051: 
022242,001052:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022243,001053: 
022244,001054:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022245,001055: 
022246,001056:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022247,001057:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022248,001058: 
022249,001059:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022250,001060: 
022251,001061:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022252,001062:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022253,001063:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022254,001064: 
022255,001065:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022256,001066: 
022257,001067:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022258,001068: 
022259,001069:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022260,001070: 
022261,001071:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022262,001072: 
022263,001073:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED -
022264,001074: 
022265,001075:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)

022267,001077: 24,3137     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022268,001078: 24,3137                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022269,001079: 24,3137           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG

022314,001124:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022315,001125:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022316,001126: 
022317,001127:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
022318,001128:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022319,001129: 
022320,001130:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022321,001131: 
022322,001132:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022323,001133:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022324,001134:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022325,001135: 
022326,001136:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022327,001137: 
022328,001138:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022329,001139:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022330,001140:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022331,001141:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022332,001142: 
022333,001143:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022334,001144: 
022335,001145:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022336,001146:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022337,001147:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022338,001148: 
022339,001149:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
022340,001150: 
022341,001151:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022342,001152:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022343,001153:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022344,001154: 
022345,001155:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022346,001156: 
022347,001157:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022348,001158: 
022349,001159:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022350,001160: 
022351,001161:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022352,001162: 
022353,001163:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022354,001164: 
022355,001165:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022356,001166: 
022357,001167:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022358,001168: 
022359,001169:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022360,001170: 
022361,001171: 24,3210  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022362,001172: 24,3210                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022363,001173: 24,3210           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022364,001174: 24,3211           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022365,001175: 24,3212           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022366,001176: 24,3213           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022367,001177: 24,3214           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022368,001178: 24,3215           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022369,001179: 24,3216           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022370,001180: 24,3217           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022371,001181: 24,3220           05353        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG

022659,001469:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022660,001470: 
022661,001471:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022662,001472: 
022663,001473:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022664,001474:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022665,001475:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022666,001476:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022667,001477:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022668,001478: 
022669,001479:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022670,001480:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022671,001481:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022672,001482:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022673,001483: 
022674,001484:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022675,001485:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022676,001486:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022677,001487:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022678,001488:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022679,001489: 
022680,001490:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022681,001491: 
022682,001492:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022683,001493:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022684,001494: 
022685,001495:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022686,001496: 
022687,001497:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022688,001498:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022689,001499:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022690,001500: 
022691,001501:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022692,001502: 
022693,001503:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022694,001504: 
022695,001505:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022696,001506: 
022697,001507:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022698,001508:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022699,001509: 
022700,001510:    4523           00006        RRLIMCHK           EXTEND                                         
022701,001511:    4524           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
022702,001512:    4525           50000                           INDEX    0

022743,001553:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                 . IF EITHER:
022744,001554: 
022745,001555:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022746,001556:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.              HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022747,001557:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022748,001558:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022749,001559:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022750,001560:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022751,001561:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022752,001562:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022753,001563:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022754,001564:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022755,001565:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022756,001566:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022757,001567:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022758,001568:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022759,001569:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022760,001570:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022761,001571:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022762,001572:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022763,001573:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022764,001574:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL

022815,001625:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022816,001626: 
022817,001627:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022818,001628: 
022819,001629:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022820,001630:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022821,001631:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022822,001632:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022823,001633:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022824,001634:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022825,001635:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022826,001636:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022827,001637:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022828,001638:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022829,001639:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022830,001640:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022831,001641: 
022832,001642:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022833,001643:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022834,001644:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022835,001645: 
022836,001646:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022837,001647: 
022838,001648:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022839,001649: 
022840,001650:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022841,001651: 
022842,001652:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022843,001653:                                                                                                  #        
022844,001654:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022845,001655: 
022846,001656:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022847,001657:

022850,001660: 24,3256                                           BANK     24

022864,001674:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022865,001675: 
022866,001676:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022867,001677: 
022868,001678:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022869,001679:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022870,001680:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022871,001681:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022872,001682:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022873,001683:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022874,001684:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022875,001685:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022876,001686:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022877,001687:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022878,001688:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022879,001689:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022880,001690:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022881,001691:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022882,001692:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022883,001693: 
022884,001694:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022885,001695: 
022886,001696:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022887,001697: 
022888,001698:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022889,001699: 
022890,001700:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022891,001701:

022893,001703: 
022894,001704:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022895,001705:

022897,001707: 
022898,001708:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)

022903,001713: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022941,001751:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022942,001752: 
022943,001753:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022944,001754: 
022945,001755:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022946,001756:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022947,001757:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022948,001758:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022949,001759:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022950,001760:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022951,001761:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022952,001762:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022953,001763:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022954,001764:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022955,001765:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022956,001766:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022957,001767:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022958,001768:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022959,001769:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022960,001770:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022961,001771:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022962,001772:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022963,001773:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022964,001774:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022965,001775:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022966,001776:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022967,001777: 
022968,001778:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022969,001779: 
022970,001780:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022971,001781:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022972,001782: 
022973,001783:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022974,001784: 
022975,001785:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022976,001786: 
022977,001787:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022978,001788: 
022979,001789:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022980,001790: 
022981,001791:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022982,001792: 
022983,001793:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022984,001794: 
022985,001795:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022986,001796: 
022987,001797:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022988,001798:

023034,001844:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
023035,001845: 
023036,001846:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
023037,001847:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
023038,001848:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
023039,001849:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
023040,001850:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
023041,001851:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
023042,001852:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
023043,001853:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023044,001854:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
023045,001855:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
023046,001856:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
023047,001857:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
023048,001858:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
023049,001859:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
023050,001860:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
023051,001861:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
023052,001862:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
023053,001863:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
023054,001864:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
023055,001865:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
023056,001866: 
023057,001867:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023058,001868: 
023059,001869:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
023060,001870:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
023061,001871:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023062,001872:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
023063,001873: 
023064,001874:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023065,001875: 
023066,001876:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
023067,001877: 
023068,001878:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023069,001879:

023071,001881:

023073,001883:

023130,001940:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023131,001941: 
023132,001942:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023133,001943: 
023134,001944:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023135,001945:                                                                                                  #        RRMANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023136,001946:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023137,001947:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023138,001948:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023139,001949:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023140,001950:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023141,001951:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023142,001952:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023143,001953:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023144,001954:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023145,001955:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023146,001956:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023147,001957:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023148,001958: 
023149,001959:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023150,001960:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023151,001961:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023152,001962:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023153,001963:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023154,001964: 
023155,001965:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023156,001966: 
023157,001967:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023158,001968: 
023159,001969:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023160,001970: 
023161,001971:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023162,001972: 
023163,001973:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023164,001974: 
023165,001975:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023166,001976: 
023167,001977:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023168,001978: 
023169,001979:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_ REPOSRPT (REMODE AND REPOSITION FLAGS PRESENT - RADMODES
023170,001980:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)
023171,001981:                                                                                                  #        L+1 (ANGLE WITHIN ONE DEGREE OR RR OUT OF AUTO MODE)
023172,001982:

023222,002032:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023223,002033: 
023224,002034:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023225,002035: 
023226,002036:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023227,002037:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023228,002038:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023229,002039:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023230,002040:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023231,002041:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023232,002042:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023233,002043:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023234,002044:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023235,002045:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023236,002046:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023237,002047:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023238,002048:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023239,002049: 
023240,002050:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023241,002051:                                                                                                  #        
023242,002052:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023243,002053:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

023332,002142:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023333,002143: 
023334,002144:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023335,002145: 
023336,002146:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023337,002147:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023338,002148:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023339,002149:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023340,002150:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023341,002151:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023342,002152:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023343,002153:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023344,002154:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023345,002155:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023346,002156:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023347,002157:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023348,002158:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023349,002159:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023350,002160:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023351,002161:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023352,002162:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023353,002163:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023354,002164:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023355,002165:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023356,002166:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023357,002167:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023358,002168: 
023359,002169:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023360,002170: 
023361,002171:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023362,002172:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
023363,002173:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023364,002174:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023365,002175: 
023366,002176:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023367,002177: 
023368,002178:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023369,002179: 
023370,002180:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023371,002181: 
023372,002182:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023373,002183:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023374,002184: 
023375,002185:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023376,002186: 
023377,002187:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023378,002188: 
023379,002189:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023380,002190: 
023381,002191:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023382,002192:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
023383,002193:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                 CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.

023422,002232:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023423,002233: 
023424,002234:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023425,002235:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023426,002236:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023427,002237:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023428,002238:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023429,002239:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023430,002240:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023431,002241:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023432,002242:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023433,002243:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023434,002244:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023435,002245:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023436,002246:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023437,002247:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023438,002248:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023439,002249:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023440,002250:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023441,002251:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023442,002252:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023443,002253:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023444,002254:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.

023446,002256:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
