023595,002405:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023596,002406: 
023597,002407:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023598,002408:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023599,002409:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023600,002410:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023601,002411:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023602,002412:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023603,002413:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023604,002414:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023605,002415:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023606,002416:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023607,002417:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023608,002418:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023609,002419:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023610,002420:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023611,002421:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023612,002422:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023613,002423:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023614,002424:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023615,002425:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023616,002426:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023617,002427:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023618,002428:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023619,002429:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023620,002430:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023621,002431:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023622,002432:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023623,002433: 
023624,002434:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023625,002435: 
023626,002436:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023627,002437:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023628,002438:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023629,002439: 
023630,002440:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023631,002441:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023632,002442: 
023633,002443:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023634,002444:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023635,002445: 
023636,002446:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023637,002447: 
023638,002448:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023639,002449:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023640,002450: 
023641,002451:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023642,002452:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023643,002453:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023644,002454: 
023645,002455: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023690,002500:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023691,002501: 
023692,002502:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023693,002503: 
023694,002504:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023695,002505:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023696,002506:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023697,002507:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023698,002508:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023699,002509:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023700,002510:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023701,002511:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023702,002512:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023703,002513:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023704,002514:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023705,002515:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023706,002516:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023707,002517:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023708,002518:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023709,002519:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023710,002520:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023711,002521:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023712,002522:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023713,002523:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023714,002524:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023715,002525:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023716,002526:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023717,002527:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023718,002528:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023719,002529:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023720,002530:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023721,002531:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023722,002532:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023723,002533:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023724,002534:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023725,002535:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023726,002536:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023727,002537:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023728,002538:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023729,002539:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023730,002540:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023731,002541: 
023732,002542:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023733,002543: 
023734,002544:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023735,002545: 
023736,002546:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023737,002547: 
023738,002548:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023739,002549:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023740,002550: 
023741,002551:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023742,002552: 
023743,002553:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT

Page 552 

023745,002555: 
023746,002556:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023747,002557: 
023748,002558:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023749,002559: 
023750,002560:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023751,002561: 
023752,002562:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023753,002563:

023808,002618:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A
023809,002619:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

024427,003237:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION

024430,003240:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024431,003241:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.

024556,003366:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024557,003367:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024558,003368: 
024559,003369:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024560,003370:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024561,003371:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024562,003372:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024563,003373:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024564,003374: 
024565,003375:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024566,003376: 
024567,003377:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024568,003378:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024569,003379:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024570,003380:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024571,003381:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024572,003382: 
024573,003383:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024574,003384: 
024575,003385:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024576,003386:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024577,003387:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024578,003388: 
024579,003389:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024580,003390:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024581,003391: 
024582,003392:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024583,003393:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024584,003394: 
024585,003395:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024586,003396:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024587,003397:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024588,003398:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024589,003399:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024590,003400:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024591,003401: 
024592,003402:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024593,003403:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 575 

024595,003405:                                                                                                  #                1) RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
024596,003406:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024597,003407:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024598,003408: 
024599,003409:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  LRS22.1X, A, L, Q, PUSHLIST
024600,003410:

024729,003539:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LRS22.2 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 2)

024731,003541: 
024732,003542:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
024733,003543:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS

024740,003550:

024747,003557:                                                                                                  #        RM - RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024748,003558:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 - INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024749,003559:

024780,003590:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024781,003591:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION - P20-25
024782,003592:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                    ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024783,003593: 
024784,003594:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024785,003595:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024786,003596:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024787,003597:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024788,003598: 
024789,003599:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024790,003600:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024791,003601:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024792,003602:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024793,003603:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024794,003604:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024795,003605:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024796,003606: 
024797,003607:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024798,003608:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024799,003609:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024800,003610: 
024801,003611:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024802,003612:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024803,003613:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024804,003614:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024805,003615:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024806,003616:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024807,003617: 
024808,003618:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024809,003619:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024810,003620:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024811,003621:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024812,003622:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024813,003623:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024814,003624:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024815,003625:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024816,003626:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024817,003627:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024818,003628:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024819,003629:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024820,003630:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024821,003631:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024822,003632:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024823,003633: 
024824,003634:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024825,003635:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024826,003636:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

025217,004027: 
025218,004028:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025219,004029:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025220,004030:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025221,004031:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025222,004032: 
025223,004033:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025224,004034:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025225,004035:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025226,004036: 
025227,004037:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025228,004038:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025229,004039:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025230,004040:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025231,004041:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025232,004042:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX

Page 589 

025234,004044: 
025235,004045:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025236,004046:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS

025238,004048:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025239,004049:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025240,004050:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025241,004051:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG

025442,004252:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025443,004253:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0                     BY P VOLANTE  SDC               DATE 1-15-67
025444,004254: 
025445,004255:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025446,004256: 
025447,004257:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025448,004258:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025449,004259:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025450,004260:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025451,004261: 
025452,004262:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025453,004263: 
025454,004264:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025455,004265: 
025456,004266:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025457,004267:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025458,004268:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025459,004269:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025460,004270:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025461,004271: 
025462,004272:                                                                                                  #  EXIT - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025463,004273: 
025464,004274:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025465,004275: 
025466,004276:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) - FOR DISPLAY IN R1 -     00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025467,004277:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025468,004278:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   - FOR DISPLAY IN R2 -     ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025469,004279: 
025470,004280:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025471,004281: 
025472,004282:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025473,004283:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025474,004284: 
025475,004285:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025476,004286: 
025477,004287:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025478,004288:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025479,004289:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025480,004290:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025481,004291:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025482,004292: 
025483,004293: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025484,004294: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025485,004295: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025486,004296: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025487,004297: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

025492,004302: 26,3451           00006                           EXTEND

025695,004505:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025696,004506:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025697,004507: 
025698,004508:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025699,004509: 
025700,004510:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025701,004511:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025702,004512:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025703,004513:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025704,004514:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025705,004515:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025706,004516: 
025707,004517:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025708,004518: 
025709,004519:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025710,004520: 
025711,004521:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025712,004522:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025713,004523:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025714,004524:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025715,004525:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025716,004526:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025717,004527: 
025718,004528:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025719,004529: 
025720,004530:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025721,004531: 
025722,004532:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025723,004533:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025724,004534:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025725,004535:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025726,004536:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 600 

025728,004538: 
025729,004539:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025730,004540: 
025731,004541:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025732,004542:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025733,004543:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025734,004544:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025735,004545: 
025736,004546:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025737,004547: 
025738,004548:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025739,004549:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025740,004550:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025741,004551:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025742,004552: 
025743,004553:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025744,004554: 
025745,004555:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025746,004556: 
025747,004557:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE;  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025748,004558:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025749,004559:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025750,004560: 
025751,004561: 33,2045                                           BANK     33

025851,004661:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS THAT THE DESIGNATION IS READY FOR NEW DATA.  SETTING LOSCMFLG MAKES IT GO AWAY SO SETUP29D CAN

025857,004667: 33,2143           52255                           VAD      VSU                                   #        AND ADD THE RESULT TO R(CSM) - R TO GET

025924,004734:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025925,004735: 
025926,004736:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025927,004737:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025928,004738:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025929,004739:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025930,004740:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025931,004741: 
025932,004742:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025933,004743:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025934,004744: 
025935,004745: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025936,004746: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025937,004747: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025938,004748: 
025939,004749: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025940,004750: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025941,004751: 
025942,004752: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025943,004753: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025944,004754: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025945,004755: 
025946,004756: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025947,004757: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025948,004758: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025949,004759: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025950,004760: 
025951,004761: 32,2557           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025952,004762: 32,2560           50002                           INDEX    Q
